 ) The National Green Tribunal (NGT) paid Rs 33,000 as litigation fee to uphold the demand of Rs 40 for disclosure of information, while a senior officer in the organization instructed to give information in this regard
 Was
 kendriya soochna ayog ne is aashay kii jaankaree di he
 RTI activist RK Jain wanted to know from the NGT how many number of RTI applications he received and how many of them were disposed of, but even after the order of the first appellate authority, the Central Public Relations Officer provided information of 20 pages
 Insisted on paying 40 rupees
 paryaavaran se judi is sheersh nikaay kii khinchaai karte hue soochna ayukta shridhar archyulu ne kaha ki engiti kii ore se artiai ke jawaab main pradaan jaankaree se aisa lagata he ki vah 20 pannon kii jaanakri dene ke sambandh main 40 rupee ke apane daawey ke liye 33 hajaar rupee se adhik kharch karne ko taiyaar he, jabaki is bare main pratham apiliy praadhikaar soochna dene kaa nirdesh de chuki he
 The comments archyulu ne kaha ki sambandhit adhikariyon ko yah samajhnaa chahie ki yah raashi bharat ke logon kii he or adhikari iske trustee jaise hai, jinhen is dhanrashi ko janhit ko dhyaan main rakhte hue hi kharch karnaa chahie or yah dekhnaa chahie ki ye bekaar nahin jaae
 He directed the concerned officials to bring this order to the notice of the chairman of the NGT for necessary action
 unhone kaha, 'ayog yah sifarish karti he ki engiti ke sammanit adhyaksh, jo ucchtam nyaayalay ke purv nyaayadhish hai, jimmedaar adhikari se raashi vasuulne par vichaar kare, agar is maamle main engiti ne koi raashi kharch kii he or use engiti ke paksh main jamaa kar den
 ' artiai kaaryakarta aarake jain ne engiti se yah jaananaa chaha tha ki use kitni sankhya main artiai aavedan praapt hue or inamen se kitne kaa nipataara kiya gaya, lekin pratham apiliy praadhikaar ke aadesh ke baad bhi kendriya jan sampark adhikari ne 20 pannon kii soochna pradaan karne ke liye 40 rupee kaa bhugtan karne par jor diya
 Drawing on this apex body related to environment, Information Commissioner Sridhar Archayulu said that from the information provided by the NGT in response to the RTI, it seems that he has claimed 33 thousand for his claim of Rs 40 in respect of giving information of 20 pages
 Is willing to spend more than Rs, while the first appellate authority has given instructions to give information in this regard
 tippaniyan Archayulu said that the officials concerned should understand that this amount belongs to the people of India and the officers are like its trustees, who should spend this amount only keeping public interest in mind and see that it does not go waste
 unhone sambandhit adhikariyon ko jaruri karrwai ke liye is aadesh ko engiti ke adhyaksh ke sangyaan main laane kaa nirdesh diya

 The RSF has urged the Indian government to implement a national plan to protect journalists
 sanghathan ne chetaya he ki zyaadaatar patrakaron ko unke kaam ke liye shantipurna maane jane vaale deshon main jaanboojhkar nishaanaa banaaya gaya he
 The monitoring group said in its annual audit that 67 journalists were killed this year while performing their duties, while 43 were not dead
 iske alaava 27 gaiyr-peshewar 'citigen jarnlist' or saat anya mediakarmi bhi maare gaye hai
 The RSF report states that the killing of most journalists was the result of deliberate violence against them and this reflects the failure of media personnel to defend their initiatives
 report main sanyukt raashtra se karrwai karne kaa aahvaan kiya gaya he
 The report particularly highlights 'non-state groups', which are jihadis like Islamic State groups, to carry out atrocities against journalists
 araef ne 2014 main kaha tha ki do tihaai patrkaar jangi kshetron main maare gaye hai, jabaki 2015 main yah ekadam se vipareet he or sanstha kahati he, 'do tihaai patrkaar shantipurna deshon main maare gaye hai
 'secretary General of the RSF Christophe Deloeri said that it is very important to have a special mechanism to implement international law to protect journalists
 paris aadhaarit sanstha ne kaha ki is saal 110 patrkaar maare gaye hai, jiske liye is apaat sthiti se nipatane ke liye ek tantra kii jarurat he
 a special representative of the UN secretary-general should be appointed immediately for the protection of journalists

 The Bihar government has declared 28 districts of the state as drought-hit due to the monsoon rains in the state
 rajya mantrimandal kii baithak ke baad pradesh ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar ne kaha ki pradesh ke jin 28 jilon ko suukhaagrast ghoshit kiya gaya, vahaan kii sthiti se sambandhit ek prastaav taiyaar kar aarthik sahaayta ke liye pradhanmantri da manmohan singh ko gyaapan saunpa jayega
 Afzal Amanullah, Principal Secretary, Cabinet Secretariat Coordination Department, later told journalists that the cabinet had a total of 28 districts Gaya, Jehanabad, Aurangabad, Arwal, Nawada, Patna, Nalanda, Bhojpur, Buxar, Rohtas, Kaimur, Munger, Sheikhpura, Lakhisarai, Jamui
 Decision to declare Begusarai, Bhagalpur, Banka, Siwan, Saran, Muzaffarpur, Sitamarhi, Shivhar, Vaishali, East Champaran, Madhubani, Samastipur and Darbhanga as drought affected took
 unhone bataaya ki pradesh ke shesh 10 jilon kii nirantar samiksha kii jaayegi or aavashyaktaanusaar anya jilon ko bhi suukhaagrast ghoshit karne ke bare main nirnay liya jaayegaa
 Amanullah said that due to the miserable condition of monsoon in the state, the kharif crop, especially paddy, has fallen far short of the target, which is bound to adversely affect the yield
 unhone kaha ki jin kshetron main ropani kii gayi he vahaan bhi alp evam aniyamit varsha ke kaaran upaj par pratikul prabhaav padana nishchit he
 Afzal Amanullah said that according to the report received from the Agriculture Department, the rainfall situation in the state is very bad
 ek june se 31 july tak rajya main ausatan 508
 Only 392 against 5 mm rainfall
 8 mimi barish huyi, jo ausat se 23 pratishat kam he
 Amanullah said that due to scanty rainfall, the ground and surface water resources of the state are drying up in many parts and the reservoirs and ground water level has come down significantly
 krishi evam jal sansadhano ke atirikt sookhe kaa prabhaav pashu sansaadhan evam maanav rojgaar par bhi padane kii ashanka he
 On this occasion, Principal Secretary, Disaster Management Department Vyas Ji told that Disaster Relief Fund (CRF), State Disaster Response Fund (SDRF) and National Disaster Response Fund (NCCF) or National Disaster Response Force to deal with drought in drought prone districts (NDRF) provision of assistance will come into force with immediate effect
 unhone kaha ki adhishuchet jilon main kisaanon se sahakaarita rin, rajasav lagaan evam ses, patwan shulk, vidyut shulk jo sidhe krishi se sambandhit hon kii vasuuli vittiya varsh 2010-11 ke liye sthagit rahegi
 Vyas ji said that in the affected districts, arrangements will be made to run assistance work as per requirement for saving crops, arranging alternative agricultural work, providing means for employment, maintenance of animal resources etc

 The number of metro passengers has been recorded

 3

 5

 bhartiya rail mathura or vadodara ke bich 850 kilometre lambii rail line pareuropean train control system(itisies) label-2 kaa test karne ja rahi he
 European systems are being tried to improve the signal system as it is difficult to improve passenger safety without improving the signaling
 itisies par do hajaar karod rupaya kharch aane kaa anumaan he
 railwayetcs has already tested Label-1
 342 kilometre lambey railkhand (agra-dilli-200 kimi, chennai saurban railway-117 kimi) par is system kaa test hua he
 Under this system, there is a monitor in the engine of the train, on which the messages connected to the signal are constantly coming
 rail line ke aasapaas kuch upkaran lage hote hai jo signal ke bare main monitor tak massej bhejte hai
 This allows the driver to easily get information about the red / green signal
 kohre ke sijan main aksar train haadase hote hai kyonki driver ko signal kii sahi jaankaree nahin mil paati or vah signal jump kar jaataa he
 Due to lack of accurate information of the signal, there is a risk of overspeed of trains and there is a possibility of accident
 label-2 system ke tahat ingine main lage monitor ko radio vevs se massej milte hai lekin iskaa kharch kaaphi zyada he
 According to the data, label-2 is about 30 per cent more expensive than label-1
 railway 66 hajaar kimi lambey rail khand par signling system badalane kii taiyaari main he
